<div id="review_2426072585" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2426072585" />
    <a title="Annette" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11358898-annette"><img alt="Annette" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475048089p2/11358898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2426072585?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annette" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annette" href="/user/show/11358898-annette">Annette</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141379890" href="/book/show/37806858-undercover-princess">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2426072585" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer639400933609082787">This book was smiling at me for a while already, but I had been so clever to put it on a wishlist for a bookswap, which meant that I had to wait until I would either get it or would know for sure I wouldn't get it. But, I GOT IT and that made me so incredibly happy! <br/><br/>Just like reading the book made me very happy. The book is for sure a very light read. If you go in there for the mystery and the danger, you will probably be disappointed. If you however go in there for the friendship (or more?) bet</span>
  <span id="freeText639400933609082787" style="display:none">This book was smiling at me for a while already, but I had been so clever to put it on a wishlist for a bookswap, which meant that I had to wait until I would either get it or would know for sure I wouldn't get it. But, I GOT IT and that made me so incredibly happy! <br /><br />Just like reading the book made me very happy. The book is for sure a very light read. If you go in there for the mystery and the danger, you will probably be disappointed. If you however go in there for the friendship (or more?) between two amazing girls and the joy and horrors of being a princess, this is the perfect book for you.<br /><br />The book is clearly aimed at the younger YA readers. If it had been in Dutch, I would have made my cousin read it, because she'd love it to pieces. The language used in the book is quite easy and there's quite some tell don't show at times. I have to admit, it didn't bother me that much, because it's a princess story. I wasn't expecting a very deep, layered, complicated and high standard book to begin with.<br /><br />It's just cute and innocent and adorable. Especially Lottie and her excitement over everything at court is so endearing and I really felt for her. And I love the contrast between Ellie and Lottie, with them seeming to be so different, but they still have so much in common. I also really enjoyed the fact that the romance in this book was not even much of a plot and barely there. I didn't really miss it, because the friendships and slowly blossoming feelings were a joy to read anyway.<br /><br />I'm very curious to read the second book and I hope there will be a translation soon, so my cousin can read it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="639400933609082787" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer349049246764934801">okay I'm giving this an extra star because I'll always be a sucker for Disney princess style stories<br/><br/>but boy did I have some ISSUES<br/><br/>I HATE Jamie. I suppose towards the end he was somewhat redeemed, but he was so unnecessarily rude. <br/>Lottie was SO naive and it annoyed me so much. normally I'm okay with a bit of that in books but this was next level. so many stupid decisions were made.<br/>This whole book was also very cliched, although it is a princess story so I will forgive that. but the writing was so</span>
  <span id="freeText349049246764934801" style="display:none">okay I'm giving this an extra star because I'll always be a sucker for Disney princess style stories<br /><br />but boy did I have some ISSUES<br /><br />I HATE Jamie. I suppose towards the end he was somewhat redeemed, but he was so unnecessarily rude. <br />Lottie was SO naive and it annoyed me so much. normally I'm okay with a bit of that in books but this was next level. so many stupid decisions were made.<br />This whole book was also very cliched, although it is a princess story so I will forgive that. but the writing was so boring it was hard to get engaged<br /><br />and this is probably my biggest issue: I believe the main character is meant to be bisexual? and that was not shown AT ALL. I suppose there could be some hints, but not enough. what I'm hoping is that she's in the process of discovering her sexuality, and that it will be explored more in future books. I'll read the sequel to see if this is the case. If not though, and those few hints are meant to be bisexual representation, I am very disappointed. <br /><br />Not an awful book at all, just those things really got on my nerves.<br /><br />edit: forgot to mention that there was something to do with being trans in this book (don't want to say what because could be considered spoiler) but it was handled SO weirdly. it made me uncomfortable. I'm probably reading too much into it but thought I would mention it</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6618290553114397499">This book was exactly what I needed after the harrowing last book I read. During the first half I was completely in love with it, although then it fell a little in my eyes, but still a really good book. It went a bit fast forward in the middle I think, and twords the end it sometimes became a bit hard to follow, like you as a reader didn't get enough information to understand the storyline.   <span id="freeText6618290553114397499" style="display:none">This book was exactly what I needed after the harrowing last book I read. During the first half I was completely in love with it, although then it fell a little in my eyes, but still a really good book. It went a bit fast forward in the middle I think, and twords the end it sometimes became a bit hard to follow, like you as a reader didn't get enough information to understand the storyline. But all in all it was an amazingly cozy book that I wanted to keep reading every day, and I'm excited to read the next book! I loved Lottie as a character and I was happy to read from her perspective during the whole book, I was at first afraid it was going to switch between Lottie and Ellie throughout the story. Lottie's motto is so perfect and I really like how it summerizes her character in three words, thank you Connie for bringing life to the character of Lottie!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0yfGWGjQHz8hT6WfmRYCSmzJUkzbgAnIH2fUA8WzPfAZk7By6Av12dcKBh7OadLyDae5M4nEke7P2UL/ZFRYIQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wgH8TTQbv33L8hlSwB1SN9NhVr4bliYc8lstC24iPG0ItYpntMBVmz23utOXYoKPsg+9wUnSvjoi5bv3z8VZvA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/16360627.Connie_Glynn"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1602796161p3/16360627.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/16360627.Connie_Glynn">Connie Glynn
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
643
followers
</div>

</div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14853534678863952990"><b>Connie Glynn</b> is an English author and YouTuber. Her debut novel <i>Undercover Princess,</i> the first in <i>The Rosewood Chronicles</i>, was published in 2017. <br/> Glynn is also known for her YouTube videos on the channel Noodlerella. She provided the voice for the character Moxie Dewdrop in the UK cinema version of Dreamworks' <i>Trolls</i>.</span>

</div>
</div>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_51987874').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_51987874').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_51987874').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
